< Text>
So nice to find a place doing real Indo food and not just a general pan southeast asian hybrid style that never tastes quite right.  The nasi goreng tasted just like my Oma used to make, and the peanut sauce was perfect.  The take on beef rendang was really interesting and a great brunch item, just filling enough but not too heavy.  I definitely want to come back and try the lunch/dinner menu. Plenty of parking in the neighborhood streets nearby.  Prices are a little high but in line with other "elevated" dining experiences and the quality of the food is well worth it. They even sell their house made sambal to go, which has a lot of flavor but isn't overwhelmingly spicy.  If you've never had a chance to have real Indo food, give this place a try!<//Text>

<review>What a great experience.

I've passed by here a lot because I dine at the restaurants on Coast Highway but have never stopped in. Booked marked it for over a year.

One day I finally decided to try Dija Mara. The restaurant is not huge but more intimate and the decor is beautiful.  The atmosphere is welcoming, chic and clean.

When I walked in we were greeted and offered a table. I chose to sit towards the back because the windows were wide open and although it was the perfect weather I knew I was going to get cold since the sun was going down.

Our server, and co-owner, Simaran, was very nice and helpful on explaining the dishes to us. We were about to order a handful of items then realized our eyes were bigger than our stomach. We opt for 3 dishes.

Food:
Naasi Goreng- Fried Rice topped with a fried egf
Mie Goreng-Fried Noodles (with lap cheong)
Pork Belly with Coconut Rice

The fresh herbs and bursting flavors made me enjoy every bite of my meal.
The fried noodles were cooked perfectly. I liked that there's pieces of it that were crispy. The only negative of that dish was the oil on the bottom. But don't get me wrong  I still enjoyed it.
The Pork Belly is soft and tender with a little fat that is cooked over Japanese charcoal. It went well with the coconut rice (not heavy flavored), charred broccollini and pineapple.
Lastly, the fried rice aka Nasi Goreng had pieces of shrimp and chicken con fit. The sweet soy sauce was delcious.

Guess who served our food? The Chef! Simaran says he even grows the herbs in his garden. Wow! That caught my attention. He is detailed on presentation, flavors and kind.

Overall, a highly recommended restaurant for Indonesian aka Balinese food.< /review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNcN_fQFs-qBYYjtmPL5wAnZkQ1EW1k34mHkIgo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP0rsG3flo_VxTbcL0Jn8SwRWJv_Y-z3omH9WFs=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMlfcH-bCjvnRpVnDKRr0hIVGd4k0xLZsM2hyOu=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPhK9oSpDx9aM6pCmOqvoA6pZp-6SqYvX-tCIw5=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOrbd66irb5GWvMIyBWukDx1jTOnTrWat2rrEl9=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPvx6eg-UPMuLghbJpASdpG231E1z2ZJZyu_PkO=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOtzii9n3sn7rXfc71FU5xv-NQtr662liM35Rjf=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMdfhvvj3rSPRECJKgmaP7HtHvBFRKuT3fDAn71=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPuI1Vq9l0JcA4sQKggXJYwoi5Jx6OjcJrdBbFk=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNa88h1AVwJ7chF6BMsWqCt-vYOAc1Hryzo0t9W=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPel-i-nO-_QY9XZam3Go_Q-IUScDOgbeRoLv4G=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNYX9P3N4two6-vmtEP2m3xPimI33LOalFwB8Ut=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOMGboHZm5WLi6dCtBjHcfDPw0J1nncMnaqY8jD=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><response>None< /response><GmapID>0x80dc6e3a4ffacd19:0x58a58c2adbed2f82< /GmapID></record></dataset><record>

< text>
I gave this place three stars mostly because of the size of the meals to cost of the dish ratio. I don't know why this trend of tapas style plates keep expanding. It drives me nuts as I don't ever feel like I'm getting my money's worth.

The food at Dija Mara is really great. Fresh ingredients and everything we ordered was fantastic. HOWEVER, when I'm paying $11 for four pieces of Lamb Satay that are literally the size of my thumb its NOT worth the cost regardless how tasty it is. I could see this particular dish being a $6 dish for how small it actually is, but not $11!

We also had the tiger prawns and it consisted of four shrimp some rice and a tasty sour salad garnish. it was good and it was considerably more food than the Lamb Satay. It was just two of us for dinner and we only ordered three dishes and the bill came close to $50. Unfortunately after spending $50 we weren't even full but we had maxed out our dinner budget for the evening.

I'm all for delicious food costing more, however when the size vs cost ratio doesn't match it just chaps my hide. SO I would recommend Dija Mara because the food IS delicious, however just keep in mind that they are SMALL dishes so be prepared to spend a lot more to be satiated.<//text>

< Text>
I've been here numerous times over the years and I can't believe I have yet to leave a review. I love local eateries like this. One of a kind and out of the box. This place is consistently great. Every dish is packed with flavor, but not so much that it becomes intolerable after a few bites. No, each dish is delicious to the very end; dish licking good.
The beer selection is nice, house infused liquors are made into refreshing and unique cocktails, and the wines are all natural/biodynamic (no added sulfites, no GMO yeasts, no preservatives, no chemicals, no manipulation).
Happy hour Tuesday thru Saturday from 4pm to 530pm.<//Text>

< text>
This place was decent. Two criticisms that are the reason for just 3 stars:

1)  Our beet cocktails were very light pink when other diners around us had deep purple cocktails... when I asked our server about the discrepancy she replied with "they're from a different batch." Umm... if I order a BEET cocktail it should be deep purple and if a customer asks about the discrepancy, you should replace their drink.

2)  The food was WAY TOO SALTY. Every single dish was over salted. Amazing flavors and spice level, don't get me wrong. I'd urge your kitchen staff to hold back on the salt. (I spent a month in Indonesia and can tell you that's not how salty Indonesian food is.)<//text>

< Name>
Karen Kaboth< /Name>
< Date>
1578994764109<//Date>
<rate>5</rate>< review>
WORLD CLASS! FOR FOODIES ONLY!!! Who would have guessed that you could find this in such a quaint, off-the-beaten-track, old-school dock fishing and surfer-cool town? It takes a lot of skill to find such a gem (forget mass rating sites like T, you need a natural wine app, and if you don't have one or don't love German Riesling, just stay away, please!

We don't want to give away our favorite (especially to people who don't appreciate fine dining, sharing small plates and enjoying great wines & bar drinks, with a casual atmosphere! World class! The chef and his wife own Dija Mara (lived in/are from Indonesia, modern, South-East Asia) and were incredibly personal & friendly, as was all the staff. They even surprised me with the wines (we ask them to pair and not tell us so we can try to guess) and made me their own non-alchoholic cocktail!

We will take our 3 kids there again as often as we can get all the way to Oceanside! (4,000 miles)

Sure it's not cheap nor do you load up on large, mexican-style food plates (nothing wrong with going cheap, especially if you just want a ton to eat and/or pay as little as possible).

Just sit back, relax, order some great drinks or wines, and be sure to order each and every dish!! And don't tell ANYONE! ;-) I' even embarrassed to be posting this review, but I can't help it- as grateful as I am! Chapeau, Rob & your lovely Indonesian wife!

We parents went back just the 2 of us the very next evening to order the dishes we hadn't tried yet, as well as the Nasi Goreng style noodles (unreal) and as many of the others as we could eat- all of the dishes were instant favorites, with the whole family!! We NEVER do that, but here we just had to make an exception as nothing else within 30Min radius would be nearly as satisfying and memorable.

Next time we'll try to fill the kids up on the Nasi and other carbs first, so that the fish and other sharing (tapas like) dishes don't disappear as quickly- it can be like a shark feed in our family!<//review>

< Review>
Our 2nd visit - this time for Sunday brunch. I used to live in Bali and also holidayed there many times, and throughout Asia. If you love authentic South-East Asian food, then you have to try here. There are places like this in Bali, run by young Indonesians after working in the US or Aussie food industry. Fresh design, great cocktail list, quirky takes on classic dishes. Dija Mara is a great spot for a date, but there were families packing this place out at breakfast. It has the Oceanside edginess too. Along with awesomely good Rendang and a great Nasi Lemak. We‚Äôll be regulars !< /Review>

<Gmap_id>0x80dc6e3a4ffacd19:0x58a58c2adbed2f82</Gmap_id><date>1525484454629<//date><rate>5<//rate><userid>110068206561835337461<//userid><Pictures>None</Pictures>< Review>
I love how this restaurant is contributing to the makeover of local merchants on Coast Highway. The decor and atmosphere are hip and upbeat. The menu is a real fusion, and tasty. If you are sensitive to spice, let them know up front as the authentic component of this fusion includes a level of spice. The waitress, Napua was a sweet gem and cleaned up the messy energy given by the hostess. The chef and the owner made a visit to our table and shared their inspiration. Being of Ceylonese and Indonesian culture, I  recommend trying this fusion with an open mind and enjoy! I will be back!!! Thanks for a nice experience.</Review>

<name>Mike Tomkins< /name><Gmap_id>0x80dc6e3a4ffacd19:0x58a58c2adbed2f82< /Gmap_id><Review>Great food!! Really cool to place worth checking out.<//Review></record></dataset><record>
<name>Sherrin Guy< /name>< userid>
110492630895540288292<//userid>
< Time>
1533139180432<//Time>
<rate>3< /rate>< Review>
This is a welcome alternatives to the San Diego restaurant scene, which is over saturated with gastropubs, burgers and mexican....we are in dire need of varied, delicious ethnic food! The staff barman, waiters were v pleasant, the wait was horrible half an hour turned into  1 and half hours. With such a long wait time and fairly high prices you'd think a bowl of the chips that comes round when you finally sit down would be offered but, alas no.( You cannot reserve/book). The food is fusion so the beef rendang, nasi goreng and roti kanai were much less spicy or flavorful, than versions of the Asian originals, western versions...but not bad still enjoyable. What was shocking however were the portions!! Fine dinning prices with incomparably smaller sizes than any 5 star. The Roti starter with Chicken curry equalled  one average Roti with literally 1 Tablespoon yes,  1 TBS of Curry juice in a minecule dipping bowl, not a piece of chicken flesh in sight. The mains the short rib with rice, produced 2 small short ribs with a smattering of rice..scattered around the bowl. I and my group were starving...For these prices... I'm not sure whether the cost, flavor and experience could be warranted.<//Review>

Wonderful food selection and phenomenal flavours. I think what needs to be kept in mind is that it is not an Indonesian restaurant. It is a place where southeast Asian flavours are used and fused in a beautiful way. I can‚Äôt get enough of their lunch menu (Nasi lemak with lamb skewers or beef rendang). The Mie Goreng is outstanding and the perfect start is their roti with chicken curry. I‚Äôm huge on Pandan and it is so difficult to find it here so the Pandan bread pudding is a god send. Love that everything from their breads to ice cream is made in house too! Cocktails are Super refreshing, flavourful and afforadable. The owners are wonderful and Super knowledgeable. Keep up the awesome work guys!</Review>

< review>
Fairly nice place for a walk on a trail away from traffic.  I'm from out of town and was looking for a nice place to walk in Hollister. This is the best I have found. There is a sanded / gravelled 1.2 mile loop with porta potties available every two tenths of a mile. No drinking water on site.  You can only get access to the trail from the parking area and it closes at dusk.  A lot of people walk their dogs here and even though there are signs requesting you clean up after your dog, there was a lot of dog poop right along the trail.< /review>

Initial impression was great! Has a nice walking trail around the perimeter, but then I cut through the field to get back to the car and I discovered the horror.

There are thousands of holes in the field the size of dog feet. No, not from dogs running in the mud, but from little critters.

If you let your dog run on this it's very possible for them to sprain or break an ankle or leg.

Poor planning or poor maintenance caused it to basically be unsuitable for dogs to safely play.

I thought it was suppose to be a "Dog Park"...<//Review>

< review>
We signed up on June 19th so we can use some weights. Cyrus signed us up. We paid $100 upfront. Cyrus informed us that we can freeze our account anytime since we had told him we travel a lot for work. On June 29th, I emailed their manager Maria Ramirez asking about freezing or cancelling (whichever was best). We never heard back from her. We then emailed Cyrus on July 9th regarding the same situation. Again, never heard back from him either. I ended up calling the location today, and Maria answered and I had told her what we needed to do with our accounts and I had communicated that I've been emailing Maria and Cyrus and all she said was, with an attitude "oh I've never gotten any email". Like come on you're a MANAGER, even I know that even if I didn't receive any email from a customer I would apologize maybe it was sent to a wrong email, or that it got sent to a spam folder but instead she was sooooo rude with an attitude. So I was just like whatever, just please freeze my account. Throughout the whole phone conversation she was rude, and unprofessional. Then I called again, a different person answered and I just asked to confirm her email address for me and yup, I did have the right email address. New to Elk Grove... Being an all-round smimwer, I found the pool area humongous. The lab pool is 6-ft deep throughout, 3-lane lab is sort of narrow, yet water is crystal clear. Salt filter is friendly to skin and hair, not chewing on swimsuits as quickly and badly as chlorine. At peak hour, gotta wait for a spot but generally short waits so far. I wish there is a covering roof over the lab pool as this could help the busy shady time.
Steam and sauna are spaciously adequate, yet seem on the lower end of maintenance. Some walk right in with shoes despite the posted signs. Soil, brownish stains seen on the steam room floor and window frame. Contaminated steam already caused an health issue at an LA fitness which was forced closed. FYI.
Not much into lifting... The equipment floor is spiffy. Clean, neat, vibrant possibly in parts due to clean, neat,  vibrant younger members day in day out (lol)
Kind of pricey membership fee yet generally worth the great, friendly service guys and girls and the provided amenities.
The best is saved for last... In the categories of friendliness and effectiveness, Andrew Arrieta - the sales manager - is exceling. His working attitude is awesome. <name>Peter Xaymountry</name>< Review>
My girlfriend and I stopped by here after going to Home Depot. She really like their Salmon Veggie Bowl and has been craving it for a while. So when we were at Home Depot I told her to call and place our orders so it would be quicker for us. I got the Chicken Teriyaki Bowl. They weren't really busy and dine-in is closed due to covid. They also had a notice that they won't have any coins because of the shortage and that mask is required. We didn't have to wait long when we went in to pay for our food. Basically by the time we got to the cashier and paid, the food was done. I thought my dish was okay but my girlfriend really loved her Salmon Bowl. Since this place is in a big plaza you will never have an issue finding parking.<//Review>

<text>Awful, winery absolutely never going there again. My friend (former tasting manager) highly recommended it so we went. Apparently this winery is hurting for money as their tasting room manager and staff keep track of every wine glass they give with each tasting and charge you it if it's not returned after you leave the winery. You get no warning nor does it say anywhere if you take the glass that they will charge you for it so you don't know they do it unless you check your transactions. A wedding party was having their rehearsal was finishing up while we were there and once they left one of the staff complained to the tasting manager that they took 6 glasses and his response was "don't worry we'll charge the bride for them." Mind you this couple is spending thousands of dollars at their winery and they're going to charge the bride unknownly for all those glasses. Not cool and distasteful on their part and wonder if that's even legal to charge you after you leave especially when they no longer have your credit card? The tasting manager (the only one pouring) also took a long phone call while we were there which was rude and he completely forgot about us once another couple came in that was a lot younger (there were only 4 customers total doing the tasting).
